# 3 "hash_func.c" 2



#define WSZ 256
#define HSZ 8191

int h(char *p, int m)
{
    int flip = 0;
    int len = 0;
    int s = 0;
    int shortcnt = 0;
    unsigned short *sp = ((void *)0);

    len = strnlen(p, 256);
    shortcnt = len / 2;
    sp = (unsigned short *)p;
    unsigned short hval = 0x5ab6;


    for (s = 0; s < shortcnt; s++)
    {
        unsigned short newv;
        newv = *sp;
        if (flip)
        {
            newv <<= 1;
        }
        flip = !(flip);
        hval ^= newv;
        sp++;
    }

    if (len & 0x0001)
    {
        hval ^= ((((short)(p[len-1])) << 8) | (short)(p[len-1]));
    }
    return (int)hval % m;
}

int main(int argc, char **argv) {

    hash_table *hash;

    stats_table *stats = calloc(1, sizeof(stats_table));

    char *book1;
    char *book2;
    int c;

    if (argc == 1) {
        printf("Please use this format './prog4 -d book1 -f book2'\n");
        exit(1);
    }


    while ((c = getopt(argc, argv, "d:f:")) != -1) {

        switch(c) {

            case 'd':
               book1 = optarg;
                break;

            case 'f':
                book2 = optarg;
                break;

            case '?':
                printf("\nError using flag\n");
                return(1);

            default:
                abort();
        }
    }


    hash = hash_init();


    parse_file(book1, hash, 0, stats);
    parse_file(book2, hash, 1, stats);



return 0;

}

void parse_file(char *filename, hash_table *hash, int book_num, stats_table *stats)
{
    FILE *fpt;
    char *buf = ((void *)0);
    size_t bufsize = 128;

    book_word *found_word;
    book_word *temp_word;

    temp_word = (book_word *)malloc(sizeof(book_word));

    buf = (char *)malloc(bufsize * sizeof(char));
    if (buf == ((void *)0)) {
        printf("\nUnable to allocate buffer\n");
        exit(1);
    }

    if ((fpt = fopen(filename, "r")) == ((void *)0)) {
        printf("Cannot Read from File \"%s\"\n", filename);
        exit (1);
    }




    while (getline(&buf, &bufsize, fpt) != -1) {
        printf("%s", buf);


        temp_word->word = buf;
        temp_word->count[0] = 0;
        temp_word->count[1] = 0;
        temp_word->len = strlen(buf);

        hash_val = h(temp_word->word, 8191);

        found_word = hash_search(hash, temp_word->word);

        if (found_word == ((void *)0)) {


            temp_word->count[book_num] = 1;
            hash_insert(hash, buf, temp_word);

        }

        else {

            found_word->count[book_num]++;
        }


        if (book_num == 0) {
            stats->drac_word_count++;
        }
        else if (book_num == 1) {
            stats->frank_word_count++;
        }

        stats->com_word_count++;

    }

    fclose(fpt);

}

#define WSZ 256
#define HSZ 8191

int h(char *p, int m)
{
    int flip = 0;
    int len = 0;
    int s = 0;
    int shortcnt = 0;
    unsigned short *sp = ((void *)0);

    len = strnlen(p, 256);
    shortcnt = len / 2;
    sp = (unsigned short *)p;
    unsigned short hval = 0x5ab6;


    for (s = 0; s < shortcnt; s++)
    {
        unsigned short newv;
        newv = *sp;
        if (flip)
        {
            newv <<= 1;
        }
        flip = !(flip);
        hval ^= newv;
        sp++;
    }

    if (len & 0x0001)
    {
        hval ^= ((((short)(p[len-1])) << 8) | (short)(p[len-1]));
    }
    return (int)hval % m;
}

hash_table *hash_init() {

    int init = 0;


    hash_table *hash;
    hash = (hash_table *)malloc(sizeof(hash_table));
    if (hash == ((void *)0)) {
        free(hash);
        return ((void *)0);
    }
    else {


        list *tab;
        tab = (list *)malloc(sizeof(list * 8191));

            hash->table = tab;

        for (init = 0; init < 8191 +1; init++) {
            hash->table[init] = list_init();
        }

        return(hash);

    }
}


int hash_insert(struct hash_table *ha, char *key, void *data) {

    int hash;
    book_word *word;


    hash = h(key, 8191);

    word = list_append(ha->table[hash], data);

    return 0;
}



void *hash_search(struct hash_table *ha, char *key) {

    int hash;
    book_word *found_word;

    hash = h(key, 8191);


    if (ha->table[hash] == ((void *)0)) {
        return (((void *)0));

    }

    found_word = list_first(ha->table[hash]);
    while (strcmp(key, found_word->word) != 0) {
        found_word = list_next(ha->table[hash]);
        if (found_word == ((void *)0)) {
            break;
        }
    }




    return (found_word);

}

# 644 "/usr/include/string.h" 3 4

# 5 "hash_func.c" 2

#define WSZ 256
#define HSZ 8191

int h(char *p, int m)
{
    int flip = 0;
    int len = 0;
    int s = 0;
    int shortcnt = 0;
    unsigned short *sp = ((void *)0);

    len = strnlen(p, 256);
    shortcnt = len / 2;
    sp = (unsigned short *)p;
    unsigned short hval = 0x5ab6;


    for (s = 0; s < shortcnt; s++)
    {
        unsigned short newv;
        newv = *sp;
        if (flip)
        {
            newv <<= 1;
        }
        flip = !(flip);
        hval ^= newv;
        sp++;
    }

    if (len & 0x0001)
    {
        hval ^= ((((short)(p[len-1])) << 8) | (short)(p[len-1]));
    }
    return (int)hval % m;
}

# 20 "list.c"
struct list {

    struct list_node *head;
    struct list_node *tail;
    struct list_node *current;
};

struct list_node {

    struct list_node *prev;
    struct list_node *next;
    struct list_data *data;

};





list list_init(void) {

    struct list *ret;
    ret = (struct list *)malloc(sizeof(struct list));
    if (ret != ((void *)0)) {
        ret->head = ((void *)0);
        return ret;
    }
    else {
        return ((void *)0);
    }

}





void list_finalize(list lst) {

    struct list_node *p = lst->head;
    struct list_node *t;

    if (lst->head == ((void *)0)) {
        free(lst);
    }
    else {
        while(t) {
            t = p;
            p = p->next;
            free(t);
            if (p == ((void *)0)) {
                 break;
            }
            }

        free(lst);
    }
# 91 "list.c"
}
# 104 "list.c"
list_data list_insert(list lst, list_data data) {
# 114 "list.c"
    struct list_node *insert;
    insert = (struct list_node *)malloc(sizeof(struct list_node));



    if (data == ((void *)0)) {

        free(insert);
        return(((void *)0));
    }

    else if ((lst->head == ((void *)0)) && (data != ((void *)0))) {

        insert->data = data;
        insert->next = ((void *)0);
        insert->prev = ((void *)0);
        lst->head = insert;
        lst->tail = insert;
        lst->current = insert;

        return (insert->data);

    } else if (data != ((void *)0)) {

        insert->data = data;
        insert->next = lst->head;
        lst->head->prev = insert;
        insert->prev = ((void *)0);
        lst->head = insert;
        lst->current = insert;


        return (insert->data);

    } else {

        free(insert);
        return ((void *)0);
    }


}
# 168 "list.c"
list_data list_append(list lst, list_data data) {





    struct list_node *insert;
    insert = (struct list_node *)malloc(sizeof(struct list_node));

    if (data == ((void *)0)) {

        free(insert);
        return(((void *)0));
    }

    else if ((lst->head == ((void *)0)) && (data != ((void *)0))){

        insert->data = data;
        insert->next = ((void *)0);
        insert->prev = ((void *)0);
        lst->head = insert;
        lst->tail = insert;
        lst->current = insert;

        return (insert->data);
    }

    else if ((data != ((void *)0)) && (lst->tail != ((void *)0))) {

        lst->tail->next = insert;
        insert->data = data;
        insert->prev = lst->tail;
        insert->next = ((void *)0);
        lst->tail = insert;

        lst->current = lst->tail;

        return (insert->data);

    }
    else {

        free(insert);
        return ((void *)0);
    }


}
# 229 "list.c"
list_data list_insert_before(list lst, list_data data) {





    struct list_node *temp;

    struct list_node *insert;
    insert = (struct list_node *)malloc(sizeof(struct list_node));

    if ((lst->current == ((void *)0)) || (lst->current->data == ((void *)0))) {

        free(insert);
        return (((void *)0));
    }

    else if (lst->head == ((void *)0)) {

        free(insert);
        return (list_insert(lst, data));
    }



    else if ((data != ((void *)0)) && (lst->current != ((void *)0)) && (lst->current == lst->head)) {

        temp = lst->head;
        insert->data = data;
        insert->next = temp;
        lst->head->prev = insert;
        insert->prev = ((void *)0);
        lst->current = insert;
        lst->head = lst->current;

        return (insert->data);

    }

    else if ((data != ((void *)0)) && (lst->current != ((void *)0))) {


        insert->data = data;
        insert->next = lst->current;
        insert->prev = lst->current->prev;
        lst->current->prev->next = insert;
        lst->current->prev = insert;
        lst->current = insert;



        return (insert->data);

    }



    else {

        free(insert);
        return ((void *)0);


    }


}
# 309 "list.c"
list_data list_insert_after(list lst, list_data data) {





    struct list_node *insert;
    insert = (struct list_node *)malloc(sizeof(struct list_node));

    if ((lst->current == ((void *)0)) || (lst->current->data ==((void *)0))) {

        free(insert);
        return (((void *)0));
    }

    else if (lst->head == ((void *)0)) {

        free(insert);
        return (list_insert(lst, data));
    }


    else if ((data != ((void *)0)) && (lst->current != ((void *)0)) && (lst->current == lst->tail)) {

        insert->data = data;
        insert->prev = lst->tail;
        lst->tail->next = insert;
        insert->next = ((void *)0);
        lst->current = insert;
        lst->tail = insert;

        return (insert->data);

    }


    else if ((data != ((void *)0)) && (lst->current != ((void *)0))) {


        insert->data = data;
        insert->prev = lst->current;
        insert->next = lst->current->next;
        lst->current->next->prev = insert;
        lst->current->next = insert;
        lst->current = insert;

        return (insert->data);

    }

    else {

        free(insert);
        return ((void *)0);
    }



}







list_data list_remove(list lst) {


    struct list_data *remove;


    struct list_node *currenttemp;



    if (lst->head == ((void *)0)) {

        return (((void *)0));
    }

    if (lst->current == ((void *)0)) {

        return (((void *)0));
    }


    else if ((lst->current == lst->head) && (lst->current == lst->tail)) {

        remove = lst->current->data;
        lst->current->prev = ((void *)0);
        lst->current->next = ((void *)0);
        free(lst->current);
        lst->current = ((void *)0);
        lst->head = ((void *)0);
        lst->tail = ((void *)0);

        return (remove);
    }


    else if ((lst->current == lst->head) && (lst->current != lst->tail)) {

        currenttemp = lst->current->next;
        remove = lst->current->data;
        lst->current->next->prev = ((void *)0);
        free(lst->current);
        lst->current = currenttemp;
        lst->head = lst->current;

        return (remove);
    }


    else if ((lst->current != lst->head) && (lst->current == lst->tail)) {

        currenttemp = lst->current->prev;
        remove = lst->current->data;
        lst->current->prev->next = ((void *)0);
        free(lst->current);
        lst->current = currenttemp;
        lst->tail = lst->current;

        return (remove);
    }


    else if ((lst->current != lst->head) && (lst->current != lst->tail)) {


        currenttemp = lst->current->next;
        remove = lst->current->data;
        lst->current->prev->next = lst->current->next;
        lst->current->next->prev = lst->current->prev;
        free(lst->current);
        lst->current = currenttemp;

        return (remove);
    }

    else {

        return (((void *)0));
    }
}







list_data list_first(list lst) {

    if (lst->head == ((void *)0)) {


        return (((void *)0));
    }

    else {
    lst->current = lst->head;

    return(lst->head->data);
    }
}
# 484 "list.c"
list_data list_next(list lst) {



    if (lst->head == ((void *)0)) {
        return (((void *)0));
    }

    if ((lst->current == ((void *)0)) || (lst->current->data == ((void *)0))) {

        return(((void *)0));
    }

    else if (lst->current == lst->tail) {

        lst->current = ((void *)0);
        return (((void *)0));
    }




    else {

        lst->current = lst->current->next;
        return (lst->current->data);
    }
}
# 521 "list.c"
list_data list_prev(list lst) {


    if (lst->current == ((void *)0)) {

        lst->current = ((void *)0);
        return(lst->current);
    }

    if (lst->current == lst->head) {

        lst->current = ((void *)0);
        return (((void *)0));
    }



    else {
        lst->current = lst->current->prev;

        return (lst->current->data);
    }
}






list_data list_last(list lst) {

    if (lst->tail == ((void *)0)) {


        return(((void *)0));
    }

    else {
        lst->current = lst->tail;
        return(lst->tail->data);
    }
}





list_data list_curr(list lst) {

    if (lst->current == ((void *)0)) {
        return (((void *)0));
    }
    else {

        return (lst->current->data);
    }


}
